<p><br>

<ul><li><b>Upload files through this page: <a href="/wiki/index.php/Special:Upload" title="Special:Upload">Special:Upload</a>.</b>
<ul><li>If you get an error or need another filetype allowed, send bernard a <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scioly.org/forums/ucp.php?i=pm&amp;mode=compose&amp;u=22093">private message</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Please <b>put what the tests are from</b> (location/tournament/year) either in the filename, the summary, or both.</li>
<li><b>PDF is the preferred format for all tests</b>, excluding PowerPoint presentations or Excel spreadsheets. If a file is not in PDF form, <b>specify in parentheses</b> what format it's in (e.g. (.docx) or (.ppt)).
<ul><li>Please <b>upload your test to the wiki instead of linking to a Google Doc</b>! A Google Doc is subject to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/link_rot" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:link rot">link rot</a> and might become unavailable if you move or delete it, while a file uploaded to the wiki will be easier to preserve.</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Do not try to overwrite other tests or remove them from the list.</b>
<ul><li>While we want to always provide users with the greatest breadth of public resources possible to ensure that all teams have adequate access to practice tests, we understand that there are situations in which the preference is to not have tests posted in a public area. If you are a tournament director or other authority and wish for a test to be removed, send bernard a <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scioly.org/forums/ucp.php?i=pm&amp;mode=compose&amp;u=22093">private message</a> with a takedown request.</li></ul></li>
<li>See the <a href="/wiki/index.php/How_to_Write_a_Practice_Test" title="How to Write a Practice Test">Practice Test Writing Guide</a> on how to write and upload homemade tests to the test exchange.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Full_Sets">Full Sets</span></h2>
<p><i><b>Note:</b> This section is only for links to full test sets. For individual tests, please see the main body of the Test Exchange below.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tournament-Released_Sets">Tournament-Released Sets</span></h3>
<p><i><b>The following are full test sets that have been published openly by the tournaments themselves. As this is a noble practice we wish to encourage, please use these resources only for training. While we would ask prospective event supervisors to refrain from copying any of the tests on this exchange for use in a competitive setting, this request is especially important for these full sets.</b></i>
</p>

<h3><span id="&quot;Do_Not_Post&quot;"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".22Do_Not_Post.22">"Do Not Post"</span></h3>
<p>These tournaments have submitted takedown requests for test sets that have previously been posted. Keywords are used to describe when these sets can be posted: "AFTER" means only after the national tournament for that season, and "NEVER" means these test sets should never be posted to this Test Exchange.
</p>
<dl><dd>Long Island Science Olympiad (LISO) Invitational (B/C) -- NEVER -- added November 10, 2019</dd></dl>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="User-Submitted_Sets">User-Submitted Sets</span></h3>
<p><i><b>The following are test sets that have been submitted by our userbase to contribute to the resource bank available to the community.</b></i> Please assume that all contributions to this section have been done in good faith, with no malicious intent. <b>If you are a director of a tournament whose tests are found here, and you wish for the link to be removed, please send a private message <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scioly.org/forums/ucp.php?i=pm&amp;mode=compose&amp;g=5">to the administrators</a> and/or <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scioly.org/forums/ucp.php?i=pm&amp;mode=compose&amp;g=5">to the moderators</a>, and they will remove the link. Please do not remove a test yourself.</b>
</p><p>All submitted tests are subject to the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scioly.org/rules">Science Olympiad Student Center Site Rules and Policies</a>.
</p>
<dl><dd><b>Division B/C</b>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Full_Sets">Full Sets</span></h2>
<p><i><b>Note:</b> This section is only for links to full test sets. For individual tests, please see the main body of the Test Exchange below.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tournament-Released_Sets">Tournament-Released Sets</span></h3>
<p><i><b>The following are full test sets that have been published openly by the tournaments themselves. As this is a noble practice we wish to encourage, please use these resources only for training. While we would ask prospective event supervisors to refrain from copying any of the tests on this exchange for use in a competitive setting, this request is especially important for these full sets.</b></i>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="User-Submitted_Sets">User-Submitted Sets</span></h3>
<p><i><b>The following are test sets that have been submitted by our userbase to contribute to the resource bank available to the community.</b></i> Please assume that all contributions to this section have been done in good faith, with no malicious intent. <b>If you are a director of a tournament whose tests are found here, and you wish for the link to be removed, please send a private message <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scioly.org/forums/ucp.php?i=pm&amp;mode=compose&amp;g=5">to the administrators</a> or <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scioly.org/forums/ucp.php?i=pm&amp;mode=compose&amp;g=5">to the moderators</a>, and they will remove the link. Please do not remove a test yourself.</b>
</p>

<h3><span id="Climate_Change_Processes_(2009,_2017,_2018,_2022)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate_Change_Processes_.282009.2C_2017.2C_2018.2C_2022.29">Climate Change Processes (2009, 2017, 2018, 2022)</span></h3>
